msg:The hotel was formerly a hotel called "Yujiang Hotel", which joined IHG at the end of 23.
As far as the experience of this stay is concerned, it does not meet the hotel level of Crowne Plaza, as detailed below:
Check-in upgrade: The front desk staff did not mention it proactively, and upgraded to a suite after asking;
Check-in welcome: No IHG member welcome fruit was provided after the upgrade;

Breaking news:
The hotel took a shower in the room normally after swimming on the afternoon of June 6, but found that there was no hot water. I called the front desk and learned that the hot water system was under maintenance without prior notice, which was a very bad experience!

Hotel hardware:
1. Swimming pool: The door head is severely corroded, operated by a third-party agency, the water quality is acceptable, and the lockers in the locker room are not very clean;
2. Restaurant: Not experienced this time;
3. Guest room: The room decoration is relatively new Chinese style, with more ornaments, but basic supplies such as hair dryers are poor, and it has reached the "5 diamond" standard of Ctrip, but the hair dryer used is still a heating blow dryer of more than 90 yuan.
